The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	1	And Josias held the feast of the passover in Jerusalem unto his Lord,and offered the passover the fourteenth day of the first month;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	2	Having set the priests according to their daily courses,being arrayed in long garments, in the temple of the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	3	And he spake unto the Levites, the holy ministers of Israel,that they should hallow themselves unto the Lord, to setthe holy ark of the Lord in the house that king Solomonthe son of David had built:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	4	And said, Ye shall no more bear the ark upon your shoulders:now therefore serve the Lord your God, and minister unto hispeople Israel, and prepare you after your families and kindreds,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	5	According as David the king of Israel prescribed,and according to the magnificence of Solomon his son:and standing in the temple according to the several dignityof the families of you the Levites, who minister in the presenceof your brethren the children of Israel,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	6	Offer the passover in order, and make ready the sacrificesfor your brethren, and keep the passover according to thecommandment of the Lord, which was given unto Moses.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	7	And unto the people that was found there Josias gavethirty thousand lambs and kids, and three thousand calves:these things were given of the king's allowance,according as he promised, to the people, to the priests,and to the Levites.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	8	And Helkias, Zacharias, and Syelus, the governors of the temple,gave to the priests for the passover two thousand and six hundred sheep,and three hundred calves.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	9	And Jeconias, and Samaias, and Nathanael his brother, and Assabias,and Ochiel, and Joram, captains over thousands, gave to the Levitesfor the passover five thousand sheep, and seven hundred calves.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	10	And when these things were done, the priests and Levites,having the unleavened bread, stood in very comely orderaccording to the kindreds,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	11	And according to the several dignities of the fathers,before the people, to offer to the Lord, as it is writtenin the book of Moses: and thus did they in the morning.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	12	And they roasted the passover with fire, as appertaineth:as for the sacrifices, they sod them in brass pots and panswith a good savour,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	13	And set them before all the people: and afterward they preparedfor themselves, and for the priests their brethren, the sons of Aaron.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	14	For the priests offered the fat until night: and the Levitesprepared for themselves, and the priests their brethren,the sons of Aaron.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	15	The holy singers also, the sons of Asaph, were in their order,according to the appointment of David, to wit, Asaph, Zacharias,and Jeduthun, who was of the king's retinue.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	16	Moreover the porters were at every gate; it was not lawfulfor any to go from his ordinary service: for their brethrenthe Levites prepared for them.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	17	Thus were the things that belonged to the sacrificesof the Lord accomplished in that day, that they mighthold  the passover,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	18	And offer sacrifices upon the altar of the Lord,according to the commandment of king Josias.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	19	So the children of Israel which were present held thepassover at that time, and the feast of sweet bread seven days.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	20	And such a passover was not kept in Israel sincethe time of the prophet Samuel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	21	Yea, all the kings of Israel held not such a passover as Josias,and the priests, and the Levites, and the Jews, held with all Israelthat were found dwelling at Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	22	In the eighteenth year of the reign of Josias was this passover kept.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	23	And the works or Josias were upright before his Lordwith an heart full of godliness.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	24	As for the things that came to pass in his time, they were writtenin former times, concerning those that sinned, and did wickedly againstthe Lord above all people and kingdoms, and how they grieved him exceedingly,so that the words of the Lord rose up against Israel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	25	Now after all these acts of Josias it came to pass,that Pharaoh the king of Egypt came to raise war at Carchamisupon Euphrates: and Josias went out against him.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	26	But the king of Egypt sent to him, saying,What have I to do with thee, O king of Judea?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	27	I am not sent out from the Lord God against thee; for my waris upon Euphrates: and now the Lord is with me, yea, the Lord iswith me hasting me forward: depart from me, and be not against the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	28	Howbeit Josias did not turn back his chariot from him,but undertook to fight with him, not regarding the wordsof the prophet Jeremy spoken by the mouth of the Lord:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	29	But joined battle with him in the plain of Magiddo,and the princes came against king Josias.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	30	Then said the king unto his servants, Carry me away out ofthe battle; for I am very weak. And immediately his servantstook him away out of the battle.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	31	Then gat he up upon his second chariot; and being broughtback to Jerusalem died, and was buried in his father's sepulchre.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	32	And in all Jewry they mourned for Josias, yea, Jeremy the prophetlamented for Josias, and the chief men with the women made lamentationfor him unto this day: and this was given out for an ordinanceto be done continually in all the nation of Israel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	33	These things are written in the book of the stories of thekings of Judah, and every one of the acts that Josias did,and his glory, and his understanding in the law of the Lord,and the things that he had done before, and the things now recited,are reported in the book of the kings of Israel and Judea.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	34	And the people took Joachaz the son of Josias, and made him kinginstead of Josias his father, when he was twenty and three years old.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	35	And he reigned in Judea and in Jerusalem three months: andthen the king of Egypt deposed him from reigning in Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	36	And he set a tax upon the land of an hundred talentsof silver and one talent of gold.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	37	The king of Egypt also made king Joacim his brother kingof Judea and Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	38	And he bound Joacim and the nobles: but Zaraces his brotherhe apprehended, and brought him out of Egypt.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	39	Five and twenty years old was Joacim when he was made king in the landof Judea and Jerusalem; and he did evil before the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	40	Wherefore against him Nabuchodonosor the king of Babylon came up,and bound him with a chain of brass, and carried him into Babylon.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	41	Nabuchodonosor also took of the holy vessels of the Lord,and carried them away, and set them in his own temple at Babylon.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	42	But those things that are recorded of him, and of his uncleaness and impiety,are written in the chronicles of the kings.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	43	And Joacim his son reigned in his stead:he was made king being eighteen years old;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	44	And reigned but three months and ten days in Jerusalem;and did evil before the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	45	So after a year Nabuchodonosor sent and caused him to bebrought into Babylon with the holy vessels of the Lord;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	46	And made Zedechias king of Judea and Jerusalem, when he wasone and twenty years old; and he reigned eleven years:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	47	And he did evil also in the sight of the Lord, and cared notfor the words that were spoken unto him by the prophet Jeremyfrom the mouth of the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	48	And after that king Nabuchodonosor had made him to swearby the name of the Lord, he forswore himself, and rebelled;and hardening his neck, his heart, he transgressed the lawsof the Lord God of Israel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	49	The governors also of the people and of the priests did many thingsagainst the laws, and passed all the pollutions of all nations,and defiled the temple of the Lord, which was sanctified in Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	50	Nevertheless the God of their fathers sent by his messengerto call them back, because he spared them and his tabernacle also.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	51	But they had his messengers in derision; and, look, when theLord spake unto them, they made a sport of his prophets:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	52	So far forth, that he, being wroth with his people for their great ungodliness,commanded the kings of the Chaldees to come up against them;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	53	Who slew their young men with the sword, yea, even within the compassof their holy temple, and spared neither young man nor maid,old man nor child, among them; for he delivered all into their hands.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	54	And they took all the holy vessels of the Lord,both great and small, with the vessels of the ark of God,and the king's treasures, and carried them away into Babylon.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	55	As for the house of the Lord, they burnt it, and brake downthe walls of Jerusalem, and set fire upon her towers:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	56	And as for her glorious things, they never ceased till theyhad consumed and brought them all to nought: and the peoplethat were not slain with the sword he carried unto Babylon:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	57	Who became servants to him and his children, till the Persians reigned,to fulfil the word of the Lord spoken by the mouth of Jeremy:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	1	58	Until the land had enjoyed her sabbaths, the whole time of herdesolation shall she rest, until the full term of seventy years.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	1	In the first year of Cyrus king of the Persians, that theword of the Lord might be accomplished, that he had promised bythe mouth of Jeremy;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	2	The Lord raised up the spirit of Cyrus the king of thePersians, and he made proclamation through all his kingdom, andalso by writing,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	3	Saying, Thus saith Cyrus king of the Persians; The Lord ofIsrael, the most high Lord, hath made me king of the wholeworld,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	4	And commanded me to build him an house at Jerusalem in Jewry.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	5	If therefore there be any of you that are of his people, letthe Lord, even his Lord, be with him, and let him go up toJerusalem that is in Judea, and build the house of the Lord ofIsrael: for he is the Lord that dwelleth in Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	6	Whosoever then dwell in the places about, let them help him,those, I say, that are his neighbours, with gold, and withsilver,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	7	With gifts, with horses, and with cattle, and other things,which have been set forth by vow, for the temple of the Lord atJerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	8	Then the chief of the families of Judea and of the tribe ofBenjamin stood up; the priests also, and the Levites, and allthey whose mind the Lord had moved to go up, and to build anhouse for the Lord at Jerusalem,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	9	And they that dwelt round about them, and helped them in allthings with silver and gold, with horses and cattle, and withvery many free gifts of a great number whose minds were stirredup thereto.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	10	King Cyrus also brought forth the holy vessels, whichNabuchodonosor had carried away from Jerusalem, and had set upin his temple of idols.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	11	Now when Cyrus king of the Persians had brought them forth,he delivered them to Mithridates his treasurer:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	12	And by him they were delivered to Sanabassar the governor ofJudea.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	13	And this was the number of them; A thousand golden cups, anda thousand of silver, censers of silver twenty nine, vials ofgold thirty, and of silver two thousand four hundred and ten,and a thousand other vessels.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	14	So all the vessels of gold and of silver, which were carriedaway, were five thousand four hundred threescore and nine.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	15	These were brought back by Sanabassar, together with them ofthe captivity, from Babylon to Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	16	But in the time of Artexerxes king of the Persians Belemus,and Mithridates, and Tabellius, and Rathumus, and Beeltethmus,and Semellius the secretary, with others that were in commissionwith them, dwelling in Samaria and other places, wrote unto himagainst them that dwelt in Judea and Jerusalem these lettersfollowing;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	17	To king Artexerxes our lord, Thy servants, Rathumus thestorywriter, and Semellius the scribe, and the rest of theircouncil, and the judges that are in Celosyria and Phenice.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	18	Be it now known to the lord king, that the Jews that are upfrom you to us, being come into Jerusalem, that rebellious andwicked city, do build the marketplaces, and repair the walls ofit and do lay the foundation of the temple.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	19	Now if this city and the walls thereof be made up again, theywill not only refuse to give tribute, but also rebel againstkings.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	20	And forasmuch as the things pertaining to the temple are nowin hand, we think it meet not to neglect such a matter,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	21	But to speak unto our lord the king, to the intent that, ifit be thy pleasure it may be sought out in the books of thyfathers:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	22	And thou shalt find in the chronicles what is writtenconcerning these things, and shalt understand that that city wasrebellious, troubling both kings and cities:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	23	And that the Jews were rebellious, and raised always warstherein; for the which cause even this city was made desolate.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	24	Wherefore now we do declare unto thee, O lord the king, thatif this city be built again, and the walls thereof set up anew,thou shalt from henceforth have no passage into Celosyria andPhenice.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	25	Then the king wrote back again to Rathumus the storywriter,to Beeltethmus, to Semellius the scribe, and to the rest thatwere in commission, and dwellers in Samaria and Syria andPhenice, after this manner;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	26	I have read the epistle which ye have sent unto me: thereforeI commanded to make diligent search, and it hath been found thatthat city was from the beginning practising against kings;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	27	And the men therein were given to rebellion and war: and thatmighty kings and fierce were in Jerusalem, who reigned andexacted tributes in Celosyria and Phenice.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	28	Now therefore I have commanded to hinder those men frombuilding the city, and heed to be taken that there be no moredone in it;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	29	And that those wicked workers proceed no further to theannoyance of kings,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	2	30	Then king Artexerxes his letters being read, Rathumus, andSemellius the scribe, and the rest that were in commission withthem, removing in haste toward Jerusalem with a troop ofhorsemen and a multitude of people in battle array, began tohinder the builders; and the building of the temple in Jerusalemceased until the second year of the reign of Darius king of thePersians.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	1	Now when Darius reigned, he made a great feast unto all hissubjects, and unto all his household, and unto all the princesof Media and Persia,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	2	And to all the governors and captains and lieutenants thatwere under him, from India unto Ethiopia, of an hundred twentyand seven provinces.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	3	And when they had eaten and drunken, and being satisfied weregone home, then Darius the king went into his bedchamber, andslept, and soon after awaked.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	4	Then three young men, that were of the guard that kept theking's body, spake one to another;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	5	Let every one of us speak a sentence: he that shall overcome,and whose sentence shall seem wiser than the others, unto himshall the king Darius give great gifts, and great things intoken of victory:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	6	As, to be clothed in purple, to drink in gold, and to sleepupon gold, and a chariot with bridles of gold, and an headtireof fine linen, and a chain about his neck:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	7	And he shall sit next to Darius because of his wisdom, andshall be called Darius his cousin.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	8	And then every one wrote his sentence, sealed it, and laid itunder king Darius his pillow;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	9	And said that, when the king is risen, some will give him thewritings; and of whose side the king and the three princes ofPersia shall judge that his sentence is the wisest, to him shallthe victory be given, as was appointed.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	10	The first wrote, Wine is the strongest.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	11	The second wrote, The king is strongest.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	12	The third wrote, Women are strongest: but above all thingsTruth beareth away the victory.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	13	Now when the king was risen up, they took their writings, anddelivered them unto him, and so he read them:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	14	And sending forth he called all the princes of Persia andMedia, and the governors, and the captains, and the lieutenants,and the chief officers;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	15	And sat him down in the royal seat of judgment; and thewritings were read before them.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	16	And he said, Call the young men, and they shall declare theirown sentences. So they were called, and came in.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	17	And he said unto them, Declare unto us your mind concerningthe writings. Then began the first, who had spoken of thestrength of wine;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	18	And he said thus, O ye men, how exceeding strong is wine! itcauseth all men to err that drink it:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	19	It maketh the mind of the king and of the fatherless child tobe all one; of the bondman and of the freeman, of the poor manand of the rich:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	20	It turneth also every thought into jollity and mirth, so thata man remembereth neither sorrow nor debt:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	21	And it maketh every heart rich, so that a man rememberethneither king nor governor; and it maketh to speak all things bytalents:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	22	And when they are in their cups, they forget their love bothto friends and brethren, and a little after draw out swords:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	23	But when they are from the wine, they remember not what theyhave done.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	3	24	O ye men, is not wine the strongest, that enforceth to dothus? And when he had so spoken, he held his peace.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	1	Then the second, that had spoken of the strength of the king,began to say,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	2	O ye men, do not men excel in strength that bear rule oversea and land and all things in them?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	3	But yet the king is more mighty: for he is lord of all thesethings, and hath dominion over them; and whatsoever hecommandeth them they do.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	4	If he bid them make war the one against the other, they doit: if he send them out against the enemies, they go, and breakdown mountains walls and towers.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	5	They slay and are slain, and transgress not the king'scommandment: if they get the victory, they bring all to theking, as well the spoil, as all things else.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	6	Likewise for those that are no soldiers, and have not to dowith wars, but use husbundry, when they have reaped again thatwhich they had sown, they bring it to the king, and compel oneanother to pay tribute unto the king.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	7	And yet he is but one man: if he command to kill, they kill;if he command to spare, they spare;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	8	If he command to smite, they smite; if he command to makedesolate, they make desolate; if he command to build, theybuild;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	9	If he command to cut down, they cut down; if he command toplant, they plant.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	10	So all his people and his armies obey him: furthermore helieth down, he eateth and drinketh, and taketh his rest:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	11	And these keep watch round about him, neither may any onedepart, and do his own business, neither disobey they him in anything.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	12	O ye men, how should not the king be mightiest, when in suchsort he is obeyed? And he held his tongue.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	13	Then the third, who had spoken of women, and of the truth,(this was Zorobabel) began to speak.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	14	O ye men, it is not the great king, nor the multitude of men,neither is it wine, that excelleth; who is it then that ruleththem, or hath the lordship over them? are they not women?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	15	Women have borne the king and all the people that bear ruleby sea and land.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	16	Even of them came they: and they nourished them up thatplanted the vineyards, from whence the wine cometh.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	17	These also make garments for men; these bring glory unto men;and without women cannot men be.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	18	Yea, and if men have gathered together gold and silver, orany other goodly thing, do they not love a woman which is comelyin favour and beauty?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	19	And letting all those things go, do they not gape, and evenwith open mouth fix their eyes fast on her; and have not all menmore desire unto her than unto silver or gold, or any goodlything whatsoever?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	20	A man leaveth his own father that brought him up, and his owncountry, and cleaveth unto his wife.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	21	He sticketh not to spend his life with his wife. andremembereth neither father, nor mother, nor country.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	22	By this also ye must know that women have dominion over you:do ye not labour and toil, and give and bring all to the woman?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	23	Yea, a man taketh his sword, and goeth his way to rob and tosteal, to sail upon the sea and upon rivers;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	24	And looketh upon a lion, and goeth in the darkness; and whenhe hath stolen, spoiled, and robbed, he bringeth it to his love.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	25	Wherefore a man loveth his wife better than father or mother.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	26	Yea, many there be that have run out of their wits for women,and become servants for their sakes.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	27	Many also have perished, have erred, and sinned, for women.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	28	And now do ye not believe me? is not the king great in hispower? do not all regions fear to touch him?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	29	Yet did I see him and Apame the king's concubine, thedaughter of the admirable Bartacus, sitting at the right hand ofthe king,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	30	And taking the crown from the king's head, and setting itupon her own head; she also struck the king with her left hand.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	31	And yet for all this the king gaped and gazed upon her withopen mouth: if she laughed upon him, he laughed also: but if shetook any displeasure at him, the king was fain to flatter, thatshe might be reconciled to him again.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	32	O ye men, how can it be but women should be strong, seeingthey do thus?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	33	Then the king and the princes looked one upon another: so hebegan to speak of the truth.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	34	O ye men, are not women strong? great is the earth, high isthe heaven, swift is the sun in his course, for he compasseththe heavens round about, and fetcheth his course again to hisown place in one day.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	35	Is he not great that maketh these things? therefore great isthe truth, and stronger than all things.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	36	All the earth crieth upon the truth, and the heaven blessethit: all works shake and tremble at it, and with it is nounrighteous thing.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	37	Wine is wicked, the king is wicked, women are wicked, all thechildren of men are wicked, and such are all their wicked works;and there is no truth in them; in their unrighteousness alsothey shall perish.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	38	As for the truth, it endureth, and is alwaYs strong; itliveth and conquereth for evermore.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	39	With her there is no accepting of persons or rewards; but shedoeth the things that are just, and refraineth from all unjustand wicked things; and all men do well like of her works.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	40	Neither in her judgment is any unrighteousness; and she isthe strength, kingdom, power, and majesty, of all ages. Blessedbe the God of truth.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	41	And with that he held his peace. And all the people thenshouted, and said, Great is Truth, and mighty above all things.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	42	Then said the king unto him, Ask what thou wilt more than isappointed in the writing, and we will give it thee, because thouart found wisest; and thou shalt sit next me, and shalt becalled my cousin.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	43	Then said he unto the king, Remember thy vow, which thou hastvowed to build Jerusalem, in the day when thou camest to thykingdom,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	44	And to send away all the vessels that were taken away out ofJerusalem, which Cyrus set apart, when he vowed to destroyBabylon, and to send them again thither.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	45	Thou also hast vowed to build up the temple, which theEdomites burned when Judea was made desolate by the Chaldees.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	46	And now, O lord the king, this is that which I require, andwhich I desire of thee, and this is the princely liberalityproceeding from thyself: I desire therefore that thou make goodthe vow, the performance whereof with thine own mouth thou hastvowed to the King of heaven.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	47	Then Darius the king stood up, and kissed him, and wroteletters for him unto all the treasurers and lieutenants andcaptains and governors, that they should safely convey on theirway both him, and all those that go up with him to buildJerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	48	He wrote letters also unto the lieutenants that were inCelosyria and Phenice, and unto them in Libanus, that theyshould bring cedar wood from Libanus unto Jerusalem, and thatthey should build the city with him.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	49	Moreover he wrote for all the Jews that went out of his realmup into Jewry, concerning their freedom, that no officer, noruler, no lieutenant, nor treasurer, should forcibly enter intotheir doors;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	50	And that all the country which they hold should be freewithout tribute; and that the Edomites should give over thevillages of the Jews which then they held:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	51	Yea, that there should be yearly given twenty talents to thebuilding of the temple, until the time that it were built;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	52	And other ten talents yearly, to maintain the burnt offeringsupon the altar every day, as they had a commandment to offerseventeen:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	53	And that all they that went from Babylon to build the cityshould have free liberty, as well they as their posterity, andall the priests that went away.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	54	He wrote also concerning. the charges, and the priests'vestments wherein they minister;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	55	And likewise for the charges of the Levites, to be given themuntil the day that the house were finished, and Jerusalembuilded up.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	56	And he commanded to give to all that kept the city pensionsand wages.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	57	He sent away also all the vessels from Babylon, that Cyrushad set apart; and all that Cyrus had given in commandment, thesame charged he also to be done, and sent unto Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	58	Now when this young man was gone forth, he lifted up his faceto heaven toward Jerusalem, and praised the King of heaven,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	59	And said, From thee cometh victory, from thee cometh wisdom,and thine is the glory, and I am thy servant.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	60	Blessed art thou, who hast given me wisdom: for to thee Igive thanks, O Lord of our fathers.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	61	And so he took the letters, and went out, and came untoBabylon, and told it all his brethren.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	62	And they praised the God of their fathers, because he hadgiven them freedom and liberty
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	4	63	To go up, and to build Jerusalem, and the temple which iscalled by his name: and they feasted with instruments of musickand gladness seven days.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	1	After this were the principal men of the families chosenaccording to their tribes, to go up with their wives and sonsand daughters, with their menservants and maidservants, andtheir cattle.

The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	3	And all their brethren played, and he made them go uptogether with them.

The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	40	For unto them said Nehemias and Atharias, that they shouldnot be partakers of the holy things, till there arose up an highpriest clothed with doctrine and truth.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	41	So of Israel, from them of twelve years old and upward, theywere all in number forty thousand, beside menservants andwomenservants two thousand three hundred and sixty.

The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	43	Four hundred thirty and five camels, seven thousand thirtyand six horses, two hundred forty and five mules, five thousandfive hundred twenty and five beasts used to the yoke.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	44	And certain of the chief of their families, when they came tothe temple of God that is in Jerusalem, vowed to set up thehouse again in his own place according to their ability,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	45	And to give into the holy treasury of the works a thousandpounds of gold, five thousand of silver, and an hundred priestlyvestments.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	46	And so dwelt the priests and the Levites and the people inJerusalem, and in the country, the singers also and the porters;and all Israel in their villages.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	47	But when the seventh month was at hand, and when the childrenof Israel were every man in his own place, they came alltogether with one consent into the open place of the first gatewhich is toward the east.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	48	Then stood up Jesus the son of Josedec, and his brethren thepriests and Zorobabel the son of Salathiel, and his brethren,and made ready the altar of the God of Israel,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	49	To offer burnt sacrifices upon it, according as it isexpressly commanded in the book of Moses the man of God.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	50	And there were gathered unto them out of the other nations ofthe land, and they erected the altar upon his own place, becauseall the nations of the land were at enmity with them, andoppressed them; and they offered sacrifices according to thetime, and burnt offerings to the Lord both morning and evening.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	51	Also they held the feast of tabernacles, as it is commandedin the law, and offered sacrifices daily, as was meet:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	52	And after that, the continual oblations, and the sacrifice ofthe sabbaths, and of the new moons, and of all holy feasts.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	53	And all they that had made any vow to God began to offersacrifices to God from the first day of the seventh month,although the temple of the Lord was not yet built.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	54	And they gave unto the masons and carpenters money, meat, anddrink, with cheerfulness.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	55	Unto them of Zidon also and Tyre they gave carrs, that theyshould bring cedar trees from Libanus, which should be broughtby floats to the haven of Joppa, according as it was commandedthem by Cyrus king of the Persians.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	56	And in the second year and second month after his coming tothe temple of God at Jerusalem began Zorobabel the son ofSalathiel, and Jesus the son of Josedec, and their brethren, andthe priests, and the Levites, and all they that were come untoJerusalem out of the captivity:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	57	And they laid the foundation of the house of God in the firstday of the second month, in the second year after they were cometo Jewry and Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	58	And they appointed the Levites from twenty years old over theworks of the Lord. Then stood up Jesus, and his sons andbrethren, and Cadmiel his brother, and the sons of Madiabun,with the sons of Joda the son of Eliadun, with their sons andbrethren, all Levites, with one accord setters forward of thebusiness, labouring to advance the works in the house of God. Sothe workmen built the temple of the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	59	And the priests stood arrayed in their vestments with musicalinstruments and trumpets; and the Levites the sons of Asaph hadcymbals,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	60	Singing songs of thanksgiving, and praising the Lord,according as David the king of Israel had ordained.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	61	And they sung with loud voices songs to the praise of theLord, because his mercy and glory is for ever in all Israel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	62	And all the people sounded trumpets, and shouted with a loudvoice, singing songs of thanksgiving unto the Lord for therearing up of the house of the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	63	Also of the priests and Levites, and of the chief of theirfamilies, the ancients who had seen the former house came to thebuilding of this with weeping and great crying.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	64	But many with trumpets and joy shouted with loud voice,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	65	Insomuch that the trumpets might not be heard for the weepingof the people: yet the multitude sounded marvellously, so thatit was heard afar off.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	66	Wherefore when the enemies of the tribe of Judah and Benjaminheard it, they came to know what that noise of trumpets shouldmean.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	67	And they perceived that they that were of the captivity didbuild the temple unto the Lord God of Israel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	68	So they went to Zorobabel and Jesus, and to the chief of thefamilies, and said unto them, We will build together with you.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	69	For we likewise, as ye, do obey your Lord, and do sacrificeunto him from the days of Azbazareth the king of the Assyrians,who brought us hither.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	70	Then Zorobabel and Jesus and the chief of the families ofIsrael said unto them, It is not for us and you to buildtogether an house unto the Lord our God.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	71	We ourselves alone will build unto the Lord of Israel,according as Cyrus the king of the Persians hath commanded us.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	72	But the heathen of the land lying heavy upon the inhabitantsof Judea, and holding them strait, hindered their building;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	5	73	And by their secret plots, and popular persuasions andcommotions, they hindered the finishing of the building all thetime that king Cyrus lived: so they were hindered from buildingfor the space of two years, until the reign of Darius.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	1	Now in the second year of the reign of Darius Aggeus andZacharias the son of Addo, the prophets, prophesied unto theJews in Jewry and Jerusalem in the name of the Lord God ofIsrael, which was upon them.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	2	Then stood up Zorobabel the son of Salatiel, and Jesus theson of Josedec, and began to build the house of the Lord atJerusalem, the prophets of the Lord being with them, and helpingthem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	3	At the same time came unto them Sisinnes the governor ofSyria and Phenice, with Sathrabuzanes and his companions, andsaid unto them,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	4	By whose appointment do ye build this house and this roof,and perform all the other things? and who are the workmen thatperform these things?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	5	Nevertheless the elders of the Jews obtained favour, becausethe Lord had visited the captivity;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	6	And they were not hindered from building, until such time assignification was given unto Darius concerning them, and ananswer received.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	7	The copy of the letters which Sisinnes, governor of Syria andPhenice, and Sathrabuzanes, with their companions, rulers inSyria and Phenice, wrote and sent unto Darius; To king Darius,greeting:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	8	Let all things be known unto our lord the king, that beingcome into the country of Judea, and entered into the city ofJerusalem we found in the city of Jerusalem the ancients of theJews that were of the captivity
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	9	Building an house unto the Lord, great and new, of hewn andcostly stones, and the timber already laid upon the walls.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	10	And those works are done with great speed, and the work goethon prosperously in their hands, and with all glory and diligenceis it made.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	11	Then asked we these elders, saying, By whose commandmentbuild ye this house, and lay the foundations of these works?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	12	Therefore to the intent that we might give knowledge untothee by writing, we demanded of them who were the chief doers,and we required of them the names in writing of their principalmen.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	13	So they gave us this answer, We are the servants of the Lordwhich made heaven and earth.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	14	And as for this house, it was builded many years ago by aking of Israel great and strong, and was finished.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	15	But when our fathers provoked God unto wrath, and sinnedagainst the Lord of Israel which is in heaven, he gave them overinto the power of Nabuchodonosor king of Babylon, of theChaldees;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	16	Who pulled down the house, and burned it, and carried awaythe people captives unto Babylon.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	17	But in the first year that king Cyrus reigned over thecountry of Babylon Cyrus the king wrote to build up this house.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	18	And the holy vessels of gold and of silver, thatNabuchodonosor had carried away out of the house at Jerusalem,and had set them in his own temple those Cyrus the king broughtforth again out of the temple at Babylon, and they weredelivered to Zorobabel and to Sanabassarus the ruler,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	19	With commandment that he should carry away the same vessels,and put them in the temple at Jerusalem; and that the temple ofthe Lord should be built in his place.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	20	Then the same Sanabassarus, being come hither, laid thefoundations of the house of the Lord at Jerusalem; and from thattime to this being still a building, it is not yet fully ended.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	21	Now therefore, if it seem good unto the king, let search bemade among the records of king Cyrus:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	22	And if it be found that the building of the house of the Lordat Jerusalem hath been done with the consent of king Cyrus, andif our lord the king be so minded, let him signify unto usthereof.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	23	Then commanded king Darius to seek among the records atBabylon: and so at Ecbatane the palace, which is in the countryof Media, there was found a roll wherein these things wererecorded.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	24	In the first year of the reign of Cyrus king Cyrus commandedthat the house of the Lord at Jerusalem should be built again,where they do sacrifice with continual fire:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	25	Whose height shall be sixty cubits and the breadth sixtycubits, with three rows of hewn stones, and one row of new woodof that country; and the expences thereof to be given out of thehouse of king Cyrus:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	26	And that the holy vessels of the house of the Lord, both ofgold and silver, that Nabuchodonosor took out of the house atJerusalem, and brought to Babylon, should be restored to thehouse at Jerusalem, and be set in the place where they werebefore.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	27	And also he commanded that Sisinnes the governor of Syria andPhenice, and Sathrabuzanes, and their companions, and thosewhich were appointed rulers in Syria and Phenice, should becareful not to meddle with the place, but suffer Zorobabel, theservant of the Lord, and governor of Judea, and the elders ofthe Jews, to build the house of the Lord in that place.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	28	I have commanded also to have it built up whole again; andthat they look diligently to help those that be of the captivityof the Jews, till the house of the Lord be finished:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	29	And out of the tribute of Celosyria and Phenice a portioncarefully to be given these men for the sacrifices of the Lord,that is, to Zorobabel the governor, for bullocks, and rams, andlambs;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	30	And also corn, salt, wine, and oil, and that continuallyevery year without further question, according as the prieststhat be in Jerusalem shall signify to be daily spent:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	31	That offerings may be made to the most high God for the kingand for his children, and that they may pray for their lives.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	32	And he commanded that whosoever should transgress, yea, ormake light of any thing afore spoken or written, out of his ownhouse should a tree be taken, and he thereon be hanged, and allhis goods seized for the king.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	33	The Lord therefore, whose name is there called upon, utterlydestroy every king and nation, that stretcheth out his hand tohinder or endamage that house of the Lord in Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	6	34	I Darius the king have ordained that according unto thesethings it be done with diligence.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	7	1	Then Sisinnes the governor of Celosyria and Phenice, andSathrabuzanes, with their companions following the commandmentsof king Darius,

The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	7	10	And the children of Israel that were of the captivity heldthe passover the fourteenth day of the first month, after thatthe priests and the Levites were sanctified.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	7	11	They that were of the captivity were not all sanctifiedtogether: but the Levites were all sanctified together.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	7	12	And so they offered the passover for all them of thecaptivity, and for their brethren the priests, and forthemselves.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	7	13	And the children of Israel that came out of the captivity dideat, even all they that had separated themselves from theabominations of the people of the land, and sought the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	7	14	And they kept the feast of unleavened bread seven days,making merry before the Lord,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	7	15	For that he had turned the counsel of the king of Assyriatoward them, to strengthen their hands in the works of the LordGod of Israel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	1	And after these things, when Artexerxes the king of thePersians reigned came Esdras the son of Saraias, the son ofEzerias, the son of Helchiah, the son of Salum,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	2	The son of Sadduc, the son of Achitob, the son of Amarias,the son of Ezias, the son of Meremoth, the son of Zaraias, theson of Savias, the son of Boccas, the son of Abisum, the son ofPhinees, the son of Eleazar, the son of Aaron the chief priest.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	3	This Esdras went up from Babylon, as a scribe, being veryready in the law of Moses, that was given by the God of Israel.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	4	And the king did him honour: for he found grace in his sightin all his requests.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	5	There went up with him also certain of the children ofIsrael, of the priest of the Levites, of the holy singers,porters, and ministers of the temple, unto Jerusalem,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	6	In the seventh year of the reign of Artexerxes, in the fifthmonth, this was the king's seventh year; for they went fromBabylon in the first day of the first month, and came toJerusalem, according to the prosperous journey which the Lordgave them.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	7	For Esdras had very great skill, so that he omitted nothingof the law and commandments of the Lord, but taught all Israelthe ordinances and judgments.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	8	Now the copy of the commission, which was written fromArtexerxes the king, and came to Esdras the priest and reader ofthe law of the Lord, is this that followeth;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	9	King Artexerxes unto Esdras the priest and reader of the lawof the Lord sendeth greeting:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	10	Having determined to deal graciously, I have given order,that such of the nation of the Jews, and of the priests andLevites being within our realm, as are willing and desirousshould go with thee unto Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	11	As many therefore as have a mind thereunto, let them departwith thee, as it hath seemed good both to me and my sevenfriends the counsellors;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	12	That they may look unto the affairs of Judea and Jerusalem,agreeably to that which is in the law of the Lord;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	13	And carry the gifts unto the Lord of Israel to Jerusalem,which I and my friends have vowed, and all the gold and silverthat in the country of Babylon can be found, to the Lord inJerusalem,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	14	With that also which is given of the people for the temple ofthe Lord their God at Jerusalem: and that silver and gold may becollected for bullocks, rams, and lambs, and things thereuntoappertaining;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	15	To the end that they may offer sacrifices unto the Lord uponthe altar of the Lord their God, which is in Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	16	And whatsoever thou and thy brethren will do with the silverand gold, that do, according to the will of thy God.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	17	And the holy vessels of the Lord, which are given thee forthe use of the temple of thy God, which is in Jerusalem, thoushalt set before thy God in Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	18	And whatsoever thing else thou shalt remember for the use ofthe temple of thy God, thou shalt give it out of the king'streasury.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	19	And I king Artexerxes have also commanded the keepers of thetreasures in Syria and Phenice, that whatsoever Esdras thepriest and the reader of the law of the most high God shall sendfor, they should give it him with speed,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	20	To the sum of an hundred talents of silver, likewise also ofwheat even to an hundred cors, and an hundred pieces of wine,and other things in abundance.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	21	Let all things be performed after the law of God diligentlyunto the most high God, that wrath come not upon the kingdom ofthe king and his sons.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	22	I command you also, that ye require no tax, nor any otherimposition, of any of the priests, or Levites, or holy singers,or porters, or ministers of the temple, or of any that havedoings in this temple, and that no man have authority to imposeany thing upon them.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	23	And thou, Esdras, according to the wisdom of God ordainjudges and justices, that they may judge in all Syria andPhenice all those that know the law of thy God; and those thatknow it not thou shalt teach.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	24	And whosoever shall transgress the law of thy God, and of theking, shall be punished diligently, whether it be by death, orother punishment, by penalty of money, or by imprisonment.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	25	Then said Esdras the scribe, Blessed be the only Lord God ofmy fathers, who hath put these things into the heart of theking, to glorify his house that is in Jerusalem:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	26	And hath honoured me in the sight of the king, and hiscounsellors, and all his friends and nobles.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	27	Therefore was I encouraged by the help of the Lord my God,and gathered together men of Israel to go up with me.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	28	And these are the chief according to their families and severaldignities, that went up with me from Babylon in the reign ofking Artexerxes:

The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	41	And these I gathered together to the river called Theras,where we pitched our tents three days: and then I surveyed them.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	42	But when I had found there none of the priests and Levites,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	43	Then sent I unto Eleazar, and Iduel, and Masman,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	44	And Alnathan, and Mamaias, and Joribas, and Nathan, Eunatan,Zacharias, and Mosollamon, principal men and learned.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	45	And I bade them that they should go unto Saddeus the captain,who was in the place of the treasury:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	46	And commanded them that they should speak unto Daddeus, andto his brethren, and to the treasurers in that place, to send ussuch men as might execute the priests' office in the house ofthe Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	47	And by the mighty hand of our Lord they brought unto usskilful men of the sons of Moli the son of Levi, the son ofIsrael, Asebebia, and his sons, and his brethren, who wereeighteen.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	48	And Asebia, and Annus, and Osaias his brother, of the sonsof Channuneus, and their sons, were twenty men.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	49	And of the servants of the temple whom David had ordained,and the principal men for the service of the Levites to wit, theservants of the temple two hundred and twenty, the catalogue ofwhose names were shewed.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	50	And there I vowed a fast unto the young men before our Lord,to desire of him a prosperous journey both for us and them thatwere with us, for our children, and for the cattle:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	51	For I was ashamed to ask the king footmen, and horsemen, andconduct for safeguard against our adversaries.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	52	For we had said unto the king, that the power of the Lord ourGod should be with them that seek him, to support them in allways.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	53	And again we besought our Lord as touching these things, andfound him favourable unto us.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	54	Then I separated twelve of the chief of the priests,Esebrias, and Assanias, and ten men of their brethren with them:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	55	And I weighed them the gold, and the silver, and the holyvessels of the house of our Lord, which the king, and hiscouncil, and the princes, and all Israel, had given.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	56	And when I had weighed it, I delivered unto them six hundredand fifty talents of silver, and silver vessels of an hundredtalents, and an hundred talents of gold,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	57	And twenty golden vessels, and twelve vessels of brass, evenof fine brass, glittering like gold.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	58	And I said unto them, Both ye are holy unto the Lord, and thevessels are holy, and the gold and the silver is a vow unto theLord, the Lord of our fathers.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	59	Watch ye, and keep them till ye deliver them to the chief ofthe priests and Levites, and to the principal men of thefamilies of Israel, in Jerusalem, into the chambers of the houseof our God.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	60	So the priests and the Levites, who had received the silverand the gold and the vessels, brought them unto Jerusalem, intothe temple of the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	61	And from the river Theras we departed the twelfth day of thefirst month, and came to Jerusalem by the mighty hand of ourLord, which was with us: and from the beginning of our journeythe Lord delivered us from every enemy, and so we came toJerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	62	And when we had been there three days, the gold and silverthat was weighed was delivered in the house of our Lord on thefourth day unto Marmoth the priest the son of Iri.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	63	And with him was Eleazar the son of Phinees, and with themwere Josabad the son of Jesu and Moeth the son of Sabban,Levites: all was delivered them by number and weight.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	64	And all the weight of them was written up the same hour.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	65	Moreover they that were come out of the captivity offeredsacrifice unto the Lord God of Israel, even twelve bullocks forall Israel, fourscore and sixteen rams,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	66	Threescore and twelve lambs, goats for a peace offering,twelve; all of them a sacrifice to the Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	67	And they delivered the king's commandments unto the king'sstewards' and to the governors of Celosyria and Phenice; andthey honoured the people and the temple of God.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	68	Now when these things were done, the rulers came unto me, andsaid,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	69	The nation of Israel, the princes, the priests and Levites,have not put away from them the strange people of the land, northe pollutions of the Gentiles to wit, of the Canaanites,Hittites, Pheresites, Jebusites, and the Moabites, Egyptians,and Edomites.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	70	For both they and their sons have married with theirdaughters, and the holy seed is mixed with the strange people ofthe land; and from the beginning of this matter the rulers andthe great men have been partakers of this iniquity.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	71	And as soon as I had heard these things, I rent my clothes,and the holy garment, and pulled off the hair from off my headand beard, and sat me down sad and very heavy.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	72	So all they that were then moved at the word of the Lord Godof Israel assembled unto me, whilst I mourned for the iniquity:but I sat still full of heaviness until the evening sacrifice.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	73	Then rising up from the fast with my clothes and the holygarment rent, and bowing my knees, and stretching forth my handsunto the Lord,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	74	I said, O Lord, I am confounded and ashamed before thy face;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	75	For our sins are multiplied above our heads, and ourignorances have reached up unto heaven.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	76	For ever since the time of our fathers we have been and arein great sin, even unto this day.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	77	And for our sins and our fathers' we with our brethren andour kings and our priests were given up unto the kings of theearth, to the sword, and to captivity, and for a prey withshame, unto this day.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	78	And now in some measure hath mercy been shewed unto us fromthee, O Lord, that there should be left us a root and a name inthe place of thy sanctuary;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	79	And to discover unto us a light in the house of the Lord ourGod, and to give us food in the time of our servitude.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	80	Yea, when we were in bondage, we were not forsaken of ourLord; but he made us gracious before the kings of Persia, sothat they gave us food;
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	81	Yea, and honoured the temple of our Lord, and raised up thedesolate Sion, that they have given us a sure abiding in Jewryand Jerusalem.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	82	And now, O Lord, what shall we say, having these things? forwe have transgressed thy commandments, which thou gavest by thehand of thy servants the prophets, saying,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	83	That the land, which ye enter into to possess as an heritage,is a land polluted with the pollutions of the strangers of theland, and they have filled it with their uncleanness.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	84	Therefore now shall ye not join your daughters unto theirsons, neither shall ye take their daughters unto your sons.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	85	Moreover ye shall never seek to have peace with them, that yemay be strong, and eat the good things of the land, and that yemay leave the inheritance of the land unto your children forevermore.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	86	And all that is befallen is done unto us for our wicked worksand great sins; for thou, O Lord, didst make our sins light,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	87	And didst give unto us such a root: but we have turned backagain to transgress thy law, and to mingle ourselves with theuncleanness of the nations of the land.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	88	Mightest not thou be angry with us to destroy us, till thouhadst left us neither root, seed, nor name?
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	89	O Lord of Israel, thou art true: for we are left a root thisday.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	90	Behold, now are we before thee in our iniquities, for wecannot stand any longer by reason of these things before thee.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	91	And as Esdras in his prayer made his confession, weeping, andlying flat upon the ground before the temple, there gatheredunto him from Jerusalem a very great multitude of men and womenand children: for there was great weeping among the multitude.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	92	Then Jechonias the son of Jeelus, one of the sons of Israel,called out, and said, O Esdras, we have sinned against the LordGod, we have married strange women of the nations of the land,and now is all Israel aloft.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	93	Let us make an oath to the Lord, that we will put away allour wives, which we have taken of the heathen, with theirchildren,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	94	Like as thou hast decreed, and as many as do obey the law ofthe Lord.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	95	Arise and put in execution: for to thee doth this matterappertain, and we will be with thee: do valiantly.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	8	96	So Esdras arose, and took an oath of the chief of the priestsand Levites of all Israel to do after these things; and so theysware.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	1	Then Esdras rising from the court of the temple went to thechamber of Joanan the son of Eliasib,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	2	And remained there, and did eat no meat nor drink water,mourning for the great iniquities of the multitude.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	3	And there was a proclamation in all Jewry and Jerusalem toall them that were of the captivity, that they should begathered together at Jerusalem:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	4	And that whosoever met not there within two or three daysaccording as the elders that bare rule appointed, their cattleshould be seized to the use of the temple, and himself cast outfrom them that were of the captivity.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	5	And in three days were all they of the tribe of Judah andBenjamin gathered together at Jerusalem the twentieth day of theninth month.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	6	And all the multitude sat trembling in the broad court of thetemple because of the present foul weather.

The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	8	And now by confessing give glory unto the Lord God of ourfathers,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	9	And do his will, and separate yourselves from the heathen ofthe land, and from the strange women.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	10	Then cried the whole multitude, and said with a loud voice,Like as thou hast spoken, so will we do.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	11	But forasmuch as the people are many, and it is foul weather,so that we cannot stand without, and this is not a work of a dayor two, seeing our sin in these things is spread far:
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	12	Therefore let the rulers of the multitude stay, and let allthem of our habitations that have strange wives come at the timeappointed,
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	13	And with them the rulers and judges of every place, till weturn away the wrath of the Lord from us for this matter.

The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	52	For this day is holy unto the Lord: and be not sorrowful; forthe Lord will bring you to honour.
The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	53	So the Levites published all things to the people, saying,This day is holy to the Lord; be not sorrowful.
