The First Book of Esdras	1Esdr	9	55	Because they understood the words wherein they wereinstructed, and for the which they had been assembled.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	1	The second book of the prophet Esdras, the son of Saraias,the son of Azarias, the son of Helchias, the son of Sadamias,the sou of Sadoc, the son of Achitob,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	2	The son of Achias, the son of Phinees, the son of Heli,the son of Amarias, the son of Aziei, the son of Marimoth,the son of And he spake unto the of Borith, the son of Abisei,the son of Phinees, the son of Eleazar,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	3	The son of Aaron, of the tribe of Levi; which was captive inthe land of the Medes, in the reign of Artexerxes king of thePersians.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	4	And the word of the Lord came unto me, saying,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	5	Go thy way, and shew my people their sinful deeds, and theirchildren their wickedness which they have done against me; thatthey may tell their children's children:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	6	Because the sins of their fathers are increased in them: forthey have forgotten me, and have offered unto strange gods.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	7	Am not I even he that brought them out of the land of Egypt,from the house of bondage? but they have provoked me unto wrath,and despised my counsels.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	8	Pull thou off then the hair of thy head, and cast all evil upon them, for they have not been obedient unto my law, but it is a rebellious people.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	9	How long shall I forbear them, into whom I have done so much good?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	10	Many kings have I destroyed for their sakes; Pharaoh with hisservants and all his power have I smitten down.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	11	All the nations have I destroyed before them, and in the eastI have scattered the people of two provinces, even of Tyrus andSidon, and have slain all their enemies.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	12	Speak thou therefore unto them, saying, Thus saith the Lord,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	13	I led you through the sea and in the beginning gave you a large and safe passage; I gave you Moses for a leader, and Aaron for a priest.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	14	I gave you light in a pillar of fire, and great wonders haveI done among you; yet have ye forgotten me, saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	15	Thus saith the Almighty Lord, The quails were as a token to you; I gave you tents for your safeguard: nevertheless ye murmured there,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	16	And triumphed not in my name for the destruction of your enemies, but ever to this day do ye yet murmur.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	17	Where are the benefits that I have done for you? when ye werehungry and thirsty in the wilderness, did ye not cry unto me,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	18	Saying, Why hast thou brought us into this wilderness to kill us? it had been better for us to have served the Egyptians, than to die in this wilderness.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	19	Then had I pity upon your mournings, and gave you manna to eat; so ye did eat angels' bread.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	20	When ye were thirsty, did I not cleave the rock, and watersflowed out to your fill? for the heat I covered you with theleaves of the trees.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	21	I divided among you a fruitful land, I cast out theCanaanites, the Pherezites, and the Philistines, before you:what shall I yet do more for you? saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	22	Thus saith the Almighty Lord, When ye were in the wilderness,in the river of the Amorites, being athirst, and blaspheming my name,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	23	I gave you not fire for your blasphemies, but cast a tree in the water, and made the river sweet.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	24	What shall I do unto thee, O Jacob? thou, Juda, wouldest notobey me: I will turn me to other nations, and unto those will I give my name, that they may keep my statutes.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	25	Seeing ye have forsaken me, I will forsake you also; when ye desire me to be gracious unto you, I shall have no mercy upon you.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	26	Whensoever ye shall call upon me, I will not hear you: for ye have defiled your hands with blood, and your feet are swift to commit manslaughter.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	27	Ye have not as it were forsaken me, but your own selves,saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	28	Thus saith the Almighty Lord, Have I not prayed you as afather his sons, as a mother her daughters, and a nurse heryoung babes,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	29	That ye would be my people, and I should be your God; that yewould be my children, and I should be your father?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	30	I gathered you together, as a hen gathereth her chickensunder her wings: but now, what shall I do unto you? I will castyou out from my face.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	31	When ye offer unto me, I will turn my face from you: for yoursolemn feastdays, your new moons, and your circumcisions, have Iforsaken.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	32	I sent unto you my servants the prophets, whom ye have takenand slain, and torn their bodies in pieces, whose blood I willrequire of your hands, saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	33	Thus saith the Almighty Lord, Your house is desolate, I willcast you out as the wind doth stubble.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	34	And your children shall not be fruitful; for they havedespised my commandment, and done the thing that is an evilbefore me.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	35	Your houses will I give to a people that shall come; whichnot having heard of me yet shall believe me; to whom I haveshewed no signs, yet they shall do that I have commanded them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	36	They have seen no prophets, yet they shall call their sins toremembrance, and acknowledge them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	37	I take to witness the grace of the people to come, whoselittle ones rejoice in gladness: and though they have not seenme with bodily eyes, yet in spirit they believe the thing that Isay.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	38	And now, brother, behold what glory; and see the people thatcome from the east:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	39	Unto whom I will give for leaders, Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob,Oseas, Amos, and Micheas, Joel, Abdias, and Jonas,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	1	40	Nahum, and Abacuc, Sophonias, Aggeus, Zachary, and Malachy,which is called also an angel of the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	1	Thus saith the Lord, I brought this people out of bondage,and I gave them my commandments by menservants the prophets;whom they would not hear, but despised my counsels.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	2	The mother that bare them saith unto them, Go your way, yechildren; for I am a widow and forsaken.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	3	I brought you up with gladness; but with sorrow and heavinesshave I lost you: for ye have sinned before the Lord your God,and done that thing that is evil before him.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	4	But what shall I now do unto you? I am a widow and forsaken:go your way, O my children, and ask mercy of the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	5	As for me, O father, I call upon thee for a witness over themother of these children, which would not keep my covenant,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	6	That thou bring them to confusion, and their mother to aspoil, that there may be no offspring of them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	7	Let them be scattered abroad among the heathen, let theirnames be put out of the earth: for they have despised mycovenant.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	8	Woe be unto thee, Assur, thou that hidest the unrighteous inthee! O thou wicked people, remember what I did unto Sodom andGomorrha;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	9	Whose land lieth in clods of pitch and heaps of ashes: evenso also will I do unto them that hear me not, saith the AlmightyLord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	10	Thus saith the Lord unto Esdras, Tell my people that I willgive them the kingdom of Jerusalem, which I would have givenunto Israel.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	11	Their glory also will I take unto me, and give these theeverlasting tabernacles, which I had prepared for them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	12	They shall have the tree of life for an ointment of sweetsavour; they shall neither labour, nor be weary.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	13	Go, and ye shall receive: pray for few days unto you, thatthey may be shortened: the kingdom is already prepared for you:watch.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	14	Take heaven and earth to witness; for I have broken the evilin pieces, and created the good: for I live, saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	15	Mother, embrace thy children, and bring them up withgladness, make their feet as fast as a pillar: for I have chosenthee, saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	16	And those that be dead will I raise up again from theirplaces, and bring them out of the graves: for I have known myname in Israel.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	17	Fear not, thou mother of the children: for I have chosenthee, saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	18	For thy help will I send my servants Esau and Jeremy, afterwhose counsel I have sanctified and prepared for thee twelvetrees laden with divers fruits,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	19	And as many fountains flowing with milk and honey, and sevenmighty mountains, whereupon there grow roses and lilies, wherebyI will fill thy children with joy.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	20	Do right to the widow, judge for the fatherless, give to thepoor, defend the orphan, clothe the naked,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	21	Heal the broken and the weak, laugh not a lame man to scorn,defend the maimed, and let the blind man come into the sight ofmy clearness.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	22	Keep the old and young within thy walls.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	23	Wheresoever thou findest the dead, take them and bury them,and I will give thee the first place in my resurrection.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	24	Abide still, O my people, and take thy rest, for thyquietness still come.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	25	Nourish thy children, O thou good nurse; stablish their feet.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	26	As for the servants whom I have given thee, there shall notone of them perish; for I will require them from among thynumber.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	27	Be not weary: for when the day of trouble and heavinesscometh, others shall weep and be sorrowful, but thou shalt bemerry and have abundance.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	28	The heathen shall envy thee, but they shall be able to donothing against thee, saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	29	My hands shall cover thee, so that thy children shall not seehell.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	30	Be joyful, O thou mother, with thy children; for I willdeliver thee, saith the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	31	Remember thy children that sleep, for I shall bring them outof the sides of the earth, and shew mercy unto them: for I ammerciful, saith the Lord Almighty.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	32	Embrace thy children until I come and shew mercy unto them:for my wells run over, and my grace shall not fail.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	33	I Esdras received a charge of the Lord upon the mount Oreb,that I should go unto Israel; but when I came unto them, theyset me at nought, and despised the commandment of the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	34	And therefore I say unto you, O ye heathen, that hear andunderstand, look for your Shepherd, he shall give youeverlasting rest; for he is nigh at hand, that shall come in theend of the world.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	35	Be ready to the reward of the kingdom, for the everlastinglight shall shine upon you for evermore.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	36	Flee the shadow of this world, receive the joyfulness of yourglory: I testify my Saviour openly.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	37	O receive the gift that is given you, and be glad, givingthanks unto him that hath led you to the heavenly kingdom.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	38	Arise up and stand, behold the number of those that be sealedin the feast of the Lord;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	39	Which are departed from the shadow of the world, and havereceived glorious garments of the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	40	Take thy number, O Sion, and shut up those of thine that areclothed in white, which have fulfilled the law of the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	41	The number of thy children, whom thou longedst for, isfulfilled: beseech the power of the Lord, that thy people, whichhave been called from the beginning, may be hallowed.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	42	I Esdras saw upon the mount Sion a great people, whom I couldnot number, and they all praised the Lord with songs.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	43	And in the midst of them there was a young man of a highstature, taller than all the rest, and upon every one of theirheads he set crowns, and was more exalted; which I marvelled atgreatly.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	44	So I asked the angel, and said, Sir, what are these?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	45	He answered and said unto me, These be they that have put offthe mortal clothing, and put on the immortal, and have confessedthe name of God: now are they crowned, and receive palms.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	46	Then said I unto the angel, What young person is it thatcrowneth them, and giveth them palms in their hands?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	47	So he answered and said unto me, It is the Son of God, whomthey have confessed in the world. Then began I greatly tocommend them that stood so stiffly for the name of the Lord.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	2	48	Then the angel said unto me, Go thy way, and tell my peoplewhat manner of things, and how great wonders of the Lord thyGod, thou hast seen.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	1	In the thirtieth year after the ruin of the city I was inBabylon, and lay troubled upon my bed, and my thoughts came upover my heart:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	2	For I saw the desolation of Sion, and the wealth of them thatdwelt at Babylon.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	3	And my spirit was sore moved, so that I began to speak wordsfull of fear to the most High, and said,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	4	O Lord, who bearest rule, thou spakest at the beginning, whenthou didst plant the earth, and that thyself alone, andcommandedst the people,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	5	And gavest a body unto Adam without soul, which was theworkmanship of thine hands, and didst breathe into him thebreath of life, and he was made living before thee.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	6	And thou leadest him into paradise, which thy right hand hadplanted, before ever the earth came forward.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	7	And unto him thou gavest commandment to love thy way: whichhe transgressed, and immediately thou appointedst death in himand in his generations, of whom came nations, tribes, people,and kindreds, out of number.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	8	And every people walked after their own will, and didwonderful things before thee, and despised thy commandments.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	9	And again in process of time thou broughtest the flood uponthose that dwelt in the world, and destroyedst them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	10	And it came to pass in every of them, that as death was toAdam, so was the flood to these.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	11	Nevertheless one of them thou leftest, namely, Noah with hishousehold, of whom came all righteous men.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	12	And it happened, that when they that dwelt upon the earthbegan to multiply, and had gotten them many children, and were agreat people, they began again to be more ungodly than thefirst.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	13	Now when they lived so wickedly before thee, thou didstchoose thee a man from among them, whose name was Abraham.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	14	Him thou lovedst, and unto him only thou shewedst thy will:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	15	And madest an everlasting covenant with him, promising himthat thou wouldest never forsake his seed.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	16	And unto him thou gavest Isaac, and unto Isaac also thougavest Jacob and Esau. As for Jacob, thou didst choose him tothee, and put by Esau: and so Jacob became a great multitude.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	17	And it came to pass, that when thou leadest his seed out ofEgypt, thou broughtest them up to the mount Sinai.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	18	And bowing the heavens, thou didst set fast the earth,movedst the whole world, and madest the depths to tremble, andtroubledst the men of that age.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	19	And thy glory went through four gates, of fire, and ofearthquake, and of wind, and of cold; that thou mightest givethe law unto the seed of Jacob, and diligence unto thegeneration of Israel.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	20	And yet tookest thou not away from them a wicked heart, thatthy law might bring forth fruit in them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	21	For the first Adam bearing a wicked heart transgressed, andwas overcome; and so be all they that are born of him.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	22	Thus infirmity was made permanent; and the law (also) in theheart of the people with the malignity of the root; so that thegood departed away, and the evil abode still.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	23	So the times passed away, and the years were brought to anend: then didst thou raise thee up a servant, called David:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	24	Whom thou commandedst to build a city unto thy name, and tooffer incense and oblations unto thee therein.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	25	When this was done many years, then they that inhabited thecity forsook thee,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	26	And in all things did even as Adam and all his generationshad done: for they also had a wicked heart:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	27	And so thou gavest thy city over into the hands of thineenemies.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	28	Are their deeds then any better that inhabit Babylon, thatthey should therefore have the dominion over Sion?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	29	For when I came thither, and had seen impieties withoutnumber, then my soul saw many evildoers in this thirtieth year,so that my heart failed me.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	30	For I have seen how thou sufferest them sinning, and hastspared wicked doers: and hast destroyed thy people, and hastpreserved thine enemies, and hast not signified it.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	31	I do not remember how this way may be left: Are they then ofBabylon better than they of Sion?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	32	Or is there any other people that knoweth thee beside Israel?or what generation hath so believed thy covenants as Jacob?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	33	And yet their reward appeareth not, and their labour hath nofruit: for I have gone here and there through the heathen, and Isee that they flow in wealth, and think not upon thycommandments.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	34	Weigh thou therefore our wickedness now in the balance, andtheir's also that dwell the world; and so shall thy name nowhere be found but in Israel.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	35	Or when was it that they which dwell upon the earth have notsinned in thy sight? or what people have so kept thycommandments?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	3	36	Thou shalt find that Israel by name hath kept thy precepts;but not the heathen.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	1	And the angel that was sent unto me, whose name was Uriel,gave me an answer,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	2	And said, Thy heart hath gone to far in this world, andthinkest thou to comprehend the way of the most High?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	3	Then said I, Yea, my lord. And he answered me, and said, I amsent to shew thee three ways, and to set forth three similitudesbefore thee:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	4	Whereof if thou canst declare me one, I will shew thee alsothe way that thou desirest to see, and I shall shew thee fromwhence the wicked heart cometh.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	5	And I said, Tell on, my lord. Then said he unto me, Go thyway, weigh me the weight of the fire, or measure me the blast ofthe wind, or call me again the day that is past.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	6	Then answered I and said, What man is able to do that, thatthou shouldest ask such things of me?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	7	And he said unto me, If I should ask thee how great dwellingsare in the midst of the sea, or how many springs are in thebeginning of the deep, or how many springs are above thefirmament, or which are the outgoings of paradise:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	8	Peradventure thou wouldest say unto me, I never went downinto the deep, nor as yet into hell, neither did I ever climb upinto heaven.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	9	Nevertheless now have I asked thee but only of the fire andwind, and of the day wherethrough thou hast passed, and ofthings from which thou canst not be separated, and yet canstthou give me no answer of them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	10	He said moreover unto me, Thine own things, and such as aregrown up with thee, canst thou not know;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	11	How should thy vessel then be able to comprehend the way ofthe Highest, and, the world being now outwardly corrupted tounderstand the corruption that is evident in my sight?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	12	Then said I unto him, It were better that we were not at all,than that we should live still in wickedness, and to suffer, andnot to know wherefore.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	13	He answered me, and said, I went into a forest into a plain,and the trees took counsel,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	14	And said, Come, let us go and make war against the sea thatit may depart away before us, and that we may make us morewoods.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	15	The floods of the sea also in like manner took counsel, andsaid, Come, let us go up and subdue the woods of the plain, thatthere also we may make us another country.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	16	The thought of the wood was in vain, for the fire came andconsumed it.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	17	The thought of the floods of the sea came likewise to nought,for the sand stood up and stopped them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	18	If thou wert judge now betwixt these two, whom wouldest thoubegin to justify? or whom wouldest thou condemn?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	19	I answered and said, Verily it is a foolish thought that theyboth have devised, for the ground is given unto the wood, andthe sea also hath his place to bear his floods.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	20	Then answered he me, and said, Thou hast given a rightjudgment, but why judgest thou not thyself also?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	21	For like as the ground is given unto the wood, and the sea tohis floods: even so they that dwell upon the earth mayunderstand nothing but that which is upon the earth: and he thatdwelleth above the heavens may only understand the things thatare above the height of the heavens.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	22	Then answered I and said, I beseech thee, O Lord, let me haveunderstanding:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	23	For it was not my mind to be curious of the high things, butof such as pass by us daily, namely, wherefore Israel is givenup as a reproach to the heathen, and for what cause the peoplewhom thou hast loved is given over unto ungodly nations, and whythe law of our forefathers is brought to nought, and the writtencovenants come to none effect,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	24	And we pass away out of the world as grasshoppers, and ourlife is astonishment and fear, and we are not worthy to obtainmercy.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	25	What will he then do unto his name whereby we are called? ofthese things have I asked.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	26	Then answered he me, and said, The more thou searchest, themore thou shalt marvel; for the world hasteth fast to pass away,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	27	And cannot comprehend the things that are promised to therighteous in time to come: for this world is full ofunrighteousness and infirmities.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	28	But as concerning the things whereof thou askest me, I willtell thee; for the evil is sown, but the destruction thereof isnot yet come.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	29	If therefore that which is sown be not turned upside down,and if the place where the evil is sown pass not away, thencannot it come that is sown with good.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	30	For the grain of evil seed hath been sown in the heart ofAdam from the beginning, and how much ungodliness hath itbrought up unto this time? and how much shall it yet bring forthuntil the time of threshing come?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	31	Ponder now by thyself, how great fruit of wickedness thegrain of evil seed hath brought forth.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	32	And when the ears shall be cut down, which are withoutnumber, how great a floor shall they fill?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	33	Then I answered and said, How, and when shall these thingscome to pass? wherefore are our years few and evil?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	34	And he answered me, saying, Do not thou hasten above the mostHighest: for thy haste is in vain to be above him, for thou hastmuch exceeded.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	35	Did not the souls also of the righteous ask question of thesethings in their chambers, saying, How long shall I hope on thisfashion? when cometh the fruit of the floor of our reward?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	36	And unto these things Uriel the archangel gave them answer,and said, Even when the number of seeds is filled in you: for hehath weighed the world in the balance.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	37	By measure hath he measured the times; and by number hath henumbered the times; and he doth not move nor stir them, untilthe said measure be fulfilled.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	38	Then answered I and said, O Lord that bearest rule, even weall are full of impiety.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	39	And for our sakes peradventure it is that the floors of therighteous are not filled, because of the sins of them that dwellupon the earth.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	40	So he answered me, and said, Go thy way to a woman withchild, and ask of her when she hath fulfilled her nine months,if her womb may keep the birth any longer within her.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	41	Then said I, No, Lord, that can she not. And he said unto me,In the grave the chambers of souls are like the womb of a woman:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	42	For like as a woman that travaileth maketh haste to escapethe necessity of the travail: even so do these places haste todeliver those things that are committed unto them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	43	From the beginning, look, what thou desirest to see, it shallbe shewed thee.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	44	Then answered I and said, If I have found favour in thysight, and if it be possible, and if I be meet therefore,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	45	Shew me then whether there be more to come than is past, ormore past than is to come.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	46	What is past I know, but what is for to come I know not.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	47	And he said unto me, Stand up upon the right side, and Ishall expound the similitude unto thee.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	48	So I stood, and saw, and, behold, an hot burning oven passedby before me: and it happened that when the flame was gone by Ilooked, and, behold, the smoke remained still.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	49	After this there passed by before me a watery cloud, and sentdown much rain with a storm; and when the stormy rain was past,the drops remained still.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	50	Then said he unto me, Consider with thyself; as the rain ismore than the drops, and as the fire is greater than the smoke;but the drops and the smoke remain behind: so the quantity whichis past did more exceed.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	51	Then I prayed, and said, May I live, thinkest thou, untilthat time? or what shall happen in those days?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	4	52	He answered me, and said, As for the tokens whereof thouaskest me, I may tell thee of them in part: but as touching thylife, I am not sent to shew thee; for I do not know it.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	1	Nevertheless as coming the tokens, behold, the days shallcome, that they which dwell upon earth shall be taken in a greatnumber, and the way of truth shall be hidden, and the land shallbe barren of faith.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	10	And shall be sought of many, and yet not be found: then shallunrighteousness and incontinency be multiplied upon earth.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	12	At the same time shall men hope, but nothing obtain: theyshall labour, but their ways shall not prosper.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	13	To shew thee such tokens I have leave; and if thou wilt prayagain, and weep as now, and fast even days, thou shalt hear yetgreater things.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	14	Then I awaked, and an extreme fearfulness went through all mybody, and my mind was troubled, so that it fainted.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	15	So the angel that was come to talk with me held me, comfortedme, and set me up upon my feet.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	19	Then said I unto him, Go thy ways from me, and come not nighme. And he heard what I said, and went from me.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	41	And I said, Behold, O Lord, yet art thou nigh unto them thatbe reserved till the end: and what shall they do that have beenbefore me, or we that be now, or they that shall come after us?

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	43	So I answered and said, Couldest thou not make those thathave been made, and be now, and that are for to come, at once;that thou mightest shew thy judgment the sooner?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	44	Then answered he me, and said, The creature may not hasteabove the maker; neither may the world hold them at once thatshall be created therein.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	45	And I said, As thou hast said unto thy servant, that thou,which givest life to all, hast given life at once to thecreature that thou hast created, and the creature bare it: evenso it might now also bear them that now be present at once.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	46	And he said unto me, Ask the womb of a woman, and say untoher, If thou bringest forth children, why dost thou it nottogether, but one after another? pray her therefore to bringforth ten children at once.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	47	And I said, She cannot: but must do it by distance of time.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	5	51	He answered me, and said, Ask a woman that beareth children,and she shall tell thee.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	50	And that there is promised us an everlasting hope, whereasourselves being most wicked are made vain?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	51	And that there are laid up for us dwellings of health andsafety, whereas we have lived wickedly?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	52	And that the glory of the most High is kept to defend themwhich have led a wary life, whereas we have walked in the mostwicked ways of all?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	53	And that there should be shewed a paradise, whose fruitendureth for ever, wherein is security and medicine, since weshall not enter into it?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	54	(For we have walked in unpleasant places.)
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	55	And that the faces of them which have used abstinence shallshine above the stars, whereas our faces shall be blacker thandarkness?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	56	For while we lived and committed iniquity, we considered notthat we should begin to suffer for it after death.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	57	Then answered he me, and said, This is the condition of thebattle, which man that is born upon the earth shall fight;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	58	That, if he be overcome, he shall suffer as thou hast said:but if he get the victory, he shall receive the thing that Isay.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	59	For this is the life whereof Moses spake unto the peoplewhile he lived, saying, Choose thee life, that thou mayest live.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	60	Nevertheless they believed not him, nor yet the prophetsafter him, no nor me which have spoken unto them,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	61	That there should not be such heaviness in their destruction,as shall be joy over them that are persuaded to salvation.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	62	I answered then, and said, I know, Lord, that the most Highis called merciful, in that he hath mercy upon them which arenot yet come into the world,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	63	And upon those also that turn to his law;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	64	And that he is patient, and long suffereth those that havesinned, as his creatures;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	65	And that he is bountiful, for he is ready to give where itneedeth;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	66	And that he is of great mercy, for he multiplieth more andmore mercies to them that are present, and that are past, andalso to them which are to come.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	67	For if he shall not multiply his mercies, the world would notcontinue with them that inherit therein.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	68	And he pardoneth; for if he did not so of his goodness, thatthey which have committed iniquities might be eased of them, theten thousandth part of men should not remain living.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	69	And being judge, if he should not forgive them that are curedwith his word, and put out the multitude of contentions,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	7	70	There should be very few left peradventure in an innumerablemultitude.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	1	And he answered me, saying, The most High hath made thisworld for many, but the world to come for few.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	2	I will tell thee a similitude, Esdras; As when thou askestthe earth, it shall say unto thee, that it giveth much mouldwhereof earthen vessels are made, but little dust that goldcometh of: even so is the course of this present world.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	3	There be many created, but few shall be saved.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	4	So answered I and said, Swallow then down, O my soul,understanding, and devour wisdom.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	5	For thou hast agreed to give ear, and art willing toprophesy: for thou hast no longer space than only to live.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	6	O Lord, if thou suffer not thy servant, that we may praybefore thee, and thou give us seed unto our heart, and cultureto our understanding, that there may come fruit of it; how shalleach man live that is corrupt, who beareth the place of a man?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	7	For thou art alone, and we all one workmanship of thinehands, like as thou hast said.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	8	For when the body is fashioned now in the mother's womb, andthou givest it members, thy creature is preserved in fire andwater, and nine months doth thy workmanship endure thy creaturewhich is created in her.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	9	But that which keepeth and is kept shall both be preserved:and when the time cometh, the womb preserved delivereth up thethings that grew in it.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	10	For thou hast commanded out of the parts of the body, that isto say, out of the breasts, milk to be given, which is the fruitof the breasts,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	11	That the thing which is fashioned may be nourished for atime, till thou disposest it to thy mercy.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	12	Thou broughtest it up with thy righteousness, and nurturedstit in thy law, and reformedst it with thy judgment.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	13	And thou shalt mortify it as thy creature, and quicken it asthy work.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	14	If therefore thou shalt destroy him which with so greatlabour was fashioned, it is an easy thing to be ordained by thycommandment, that the thing which was made might be preserved.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	15	Now therefore, Lord, I will speak; touching man in general,thou knowest best; but touching thy people, for whose sake I amsorry;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	16	And for thine inheritance, for whose cause I mourn; and forIsrael, for whom I am heavy; and for Jacob, for whose sake I amtroubled;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	17	Therefore will I begin to pray before thee for myself and forthem: for I see the falls of us that dwell in the land.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	18	But I have heard the swiftness of the judge which is to come.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	19	Therefore hear my voice, and understand my words, and I shallspeak before thee. This is the beginning of the words of Esdras,before he was taken up: and I said,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	20	O Lord, thou that dwellest in everlastingness which beholdestfrom above things in the heaven and in the air;

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	23	Whose look drieth up the depths, and indignation maketh themountains to melt away; which the truth witnesseth:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	24	O hear the prayer of thy servant, and give ear to thepetition of thy creature.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	25	For while I live I will speak, and so long as I haveunderstanding I will answer.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	26	O look not upon the sins of thy people; but on them whichserve thee in truth.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	27	Regard not the wicked inventions of the heathen, but thedesire of those that keep thy testimonies in afflictions.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	28	Think not upon those that have walked feignedly before thee:but remember them, which according to thy will have known thyfear.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	29	Let it not be thy will to destroy them which have lived likebeasts; but to look upon them that have clearly taught thy law.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	30	Take thou no indignation at them which are deemed worse thanbeasts; but love them that always put their trust in thyrighteousness and glory.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	31	For we and our fathers do languish of such diseases: butbecause of us sinners thou shalt be called merciful.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	32	For if thou hast a desire to have mercy upon us, thou shaltbe called merciful, to us namely, that have no works ofrighteousness.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	33	For the just, which have many good works laid up with thee,shall out of their own deeds receive reward.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	34	For what is man, that thou shouldest take displeasure at him?or what is a corruptible generation, that thou shouldest be sobitter toward it?
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	35	For in truth them is no man among them that be born, but hehath dealt wickedly; and among the faithful there is none whichhath not done amiss.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	36	For in this, O Lord, thy righteousness and thy goodness shallbe declared, if thou be merciful unto them which have not theconfidence of good works.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	37	Then answered he me, and said, Some things hast thou spokenaright, and according unto thy words it shall be.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	38	For indeed I will not think on the disposition of them whichhave sinned before death, before judgment, before destruction:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	39	But I will rejoice over the disposition of the righteous, andI will remember also their pilgrimage, and the salvation, andthe reward, that they shall have.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	40	Like as I have spoken now, so shall it come to pass.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	41	For as the husbandman soweth much seed upon the ground, andplanteth many trees, and yet the thing that is sown good in hisseason cometh not up, neither doth all that is planted takeroot: even so is it of them that are sown in the world; theyshall not all be saved.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	42	I answered then and said, If I have found grace, let mespeak.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	43	Like as the husbandman's seed perisheth, if it come not up,and receive not thy rain in due season; or if there come toomuch rain, and corrupt it:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	44	Even so perisheth man also, which is formed with thy hands,and is called thine own image, because thou art like unto him,for whose sake thou hast made all things, and likened him untothe husbandman's seed.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	45	Be not wroth with us but spare thy people, and have mercyupon thine own inheritance: for thou art merciful unto thycreature.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	46	Then answered he me, and said, Things present are for thepresent, and things to cometh for such as be to come.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	47	For thou comest far short that thou shouldest be able to lovemy creature more than I: but I have ofttimes drawn nigh untothee, and unto it, but never to the unrighteous.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	50	For many great miseries shall be done to them that in thelatter time shall dwell in the world, because they have walkedin great pride.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	52	For unto you is paradise opened, the tree of life is planted,the time to come is prepared, plenteousness is made ready, acity is builded, and rest is allowed, yea, perfect goodness andwisdom.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	53	The root of evil is sealed up from you, weakness and the mothis hid from you, and corruption is fled into hell to beforgotten:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	54	Sorrows are passed, and in the end is shewed the treasure ofimmortality.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	55	And therefore ask thou no more questions concerning themultitude of them that perish.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	56	For when they had taken liberty, they despised the most High,thought scorn of his law, and forsook his ways.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	57	Moreover they have trodden down his righteous,

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	59	For as the things aforesaid shalt receive you, so thirst andpain are prepared for them: for it was not his will that menshould come to nought:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	60	But they which be created have defiled the name of him thatmade them, and were unthankful unto him which prepared life forthem.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	61	And therefore is my judgment now at hand.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	8	62	These things have I not shewed unto all men, but unto thee,and a few like thee. Then answered I and said,

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	9	5	For like as all that is made in the world hath a beginningand an end, and the end is manifest:

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	9	29	O Lord, thou that shewest thyself unto us, thou wast shewedunto our fathers in the wilderness, in a place where no mantreadeth, in a barren place, when they came out of Egypt.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	45	Whereas, I say, she said unto thee, that she hath been thirtyyears barren: those are the thirty years wherein there was nooffering made in her.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	46	But after thirty years Solomon builded the city and offeredofferings: and then bare the barren a son.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	48	But whereas she said unto thee, That my son coming into hismarriage chamber happened to have a fail, and died: this was thedestruction that came to Jerusalem.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	49	And, behold, thou sawest her likeness, and because shemourned for her son, thou begannest to comfort her: and of thesethings which have chanced, these are to be opened unto thee.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	50	For now the most High seeth that thou art grievedunfeignedly, and sufferest from thy whole heart for her, so hathhe shewed thee the brightness of her glory, and the comelinessof her beauty:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	51	And therefore I bade thee remain in the field where no housewas builded:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	52	For I knew that the Highest would shew this unto thee.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	53	Therefore I commanded thee to go into the field, where nofoundation of any building was.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	54	For in the place wherein the Highest beginneth to shew hiscity, there can no man's building be able to stand.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	55	And therefore fear not, let not thine heart be affrighted,but go thy way in, and see the beauty and greatness of thebuilding, as much as thine eyes be able to see:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	56	And then shalt thou hear as much as thine ears maycomprehend.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	10	57	For thou art blessed above many other, and art called withthe Highest; and so are but few.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	1	And it came to pass upon the third day, I sat under an oak,and, behold, there came a voice out of a bush over against me,and said, Esdras, Esdras.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	2	And I said, Here am I, Lord And I stood up upon my feet.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	3	Then said he unto me, In the bush I did manifestly revealmyself unto Moses, and talked with him, when my people served inEgypt:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	4	And I sent him and led my people out of Egypt, and broughthim up to the mount of where I held him by me a long season,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	5	And told him many wondrous things, and shewed him the secretsof the times, and the end; and commanded him, saying,

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	7	And now I say unto thee,

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	10	For the world hath lost his youth, and the times begin to waxold.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	11	For the world is divided into twelve parts, and the ten partsof it are gone already, and half of a tenth part:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	12	And there remaineth that which is after the half of the tenthpart.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	13	Now therefore set thine house in order, and reprove thypeople, comfort such of them as be in trouble, and now renouncecorruption,

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	15	And set aside the thoughts that are most heavy unto thee, andhaste thee to flee from these times.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	16	For yet greater evils than those which thou hast seen happenshall be done hereafter.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	17	For look how much the world shall be weaker through age, somuch the more shall evils increase upon them that dwell therein.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	18	For the time is fled far away, and leasing is hard at hand:for now hasteth the vision to come, which thou hast seen.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	19	Then answered I before thee, and said,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	20	Behold, Lord, I will go, as thou hast commanded me, andreprove the people which are present: but they that shall beborn afterward, who shall admonish them? thus the world is setin darkness, and they that dwell therein are without light.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	21	For thy law is burnt, therefore no man knoweth the thingsthat are done of thee, or the work that shall begin.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	22	But if I have found grace before thee, send the Holy Ghostinto me, and I shall write all that hath been done in the worldsince the beginning, which were written in thy law, that men mayfind thy path, and that they which will live in the latter daysmay live.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	23	And he answered me, saying, Go thy way, gather the peopletogether, and say unto them, that they seek thee not for fortydays.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	24	But look thou prepare thee many box trees, and take with theeSarea, Dabria, Selemia, Ecanus, and Asiel, these five which areready to write swiftly;
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	25	And come hither, and I shall light a candle of understandingin thine heart, which shall not be put out, till the things beperformed which thou shalt begin to write.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	26	And when thou hast done, some things shalt thou publish, andsome things shalt thou shew secretly to the wise: to morrow thishour shalt thou begin to write.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	27	Then went I forth, as he commanded, and gathered all thepeople together, and said,
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	28	Hear these words, O Israel.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	30	And received the law of life, which they kept not, which yealso have transgressed after them.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	31	Then was the land, even the land of Sion, parted among you bylot: but your fathers, and ye yourselves, have doneunrighteousness, and have not kept the ways which the Highestcommanded you.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	38	And the next day, behold, a voice called me, saying, Esdras,open thy mouth, and drink that I give thee to drink.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	39	Then opened I my mouth, and, behold, he reached me a fullcup, which was full as it were with water, but the colour of itwas like fire.
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	40	And I took it, and drank: and when I had drunk of it, myheart uttered understanding, and wisdom grew in my breast, formy spirit strengthened my memory:
The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	41	And my mouth was opened, and shut no more.

The Second book of Esdras	2Esdr	14	43	As for me. I spake in the day, and I held not my tongue bynight.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	52	Then many of the people were gathered unto them, to wit everyone that forsook the law; and so they committed evils in theland;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	53	And drove the Israelites into secret places, even wheresoeverthey could flee for succour.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	54	Now the fifteenth day of the month Casleu, in the hundredforty and fifth year, they set up the abomination of desolationupon the altar, and builded idol altars throughout the cities ofJuda on every side;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	55	And burnt incense at the doors of their houses, and in thestreets.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	56	And when they had rent in pieces the books of the law whichthey found, they burnt them with fire.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	57	And whosoever was found with any the book of the testament,or if any committed to the law, the king's commandment was, thatthey should put him to death.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	58	Thus did they by their authority unto the Israelites everymonth, to as many as were found in the cities.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	59	Now the five and twentieth day of the month they didsacrifice upon the idol altar, which was upon the altar of God.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	60	At which time according to the commandment they put to deathcertain women, that had caused their children to be circumcised.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	61	And they hanged the infants about their necks, and rifledtheir houses, and slew them that had circumcised them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	62	Howbeit many in Israel were fully resolved and confirmed inthemselves not to eat any unclean thing.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	63	Wherefore the rather to die, that they might not be defiledwith meats, and that they might not profane the holy covenant:so then they died.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	1	64	And there was very great wrath upon Israel.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	1	In those days arose Mattathias the son of John, the son ofSimeon, a priest of the sons of Joarib, from Jerusalem, anddwelt in Modin.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	2	And he had five sons, Joannan, called Caddis:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	3	Simon; called Thassi:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	4	Judas, who was called Maccabeus:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	5	Eleazar, called Avaran: and Jonathan, whose surname wasApphus.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	6	And when he saw the blasphemies that were committed in Judaand Jerusalem,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	7	He said, Woe is me! wherefore was I born to see this miseryof my people, and of the holy city, and to dwell there, when itwas delivered into the hand of the enemy, and the sanctuary intothe hand of strangers?
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	8	Her temple is become as a man without glory.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	9	Her glorious vessels are carried away into captivity, herinfants are slain in the streets, her young men with the swordof the enemy.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	10	What nation hath not had a part in her kingdom and gotten ofher spoils?
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	11	All her ornaments are taken away; of a free woman she isbecome a bondslave.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	12	And, behold, our sanctuary, even our beauty and our glory, islaid waste, and the Gentiles have profaned it.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	13	To what end therefore shall we live any longer?
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	14	Then Mattathias and his sons rent their clothes, and put onsackcloth, and mourned very sore.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	15	In the mean while the king's officers, such as compelled thepeople to revolt, came into the city Modin, to make themsacrifice.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	16	And when many of Israel came unto them, Mattathias also andhis sons came together.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	17	Then answered the king's officers, and said to Mattathias onthis wise, Thou art a ruler, and an honourable and great man inthis city, and strengthened with sons and brethren:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	18	Now therefore come thou first, and fulfil the king'scommandment, like as all the heathen have done, yea, and the menof Juda also, and such as remain at Jerusalem: so shalt thou andthy house be in the number of the king's friends, and thou andthy children shall be honoured with silver and gold, and manyrewards.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	19	Then Mattathias answered and spake with a loud voice, Thoughall the nations that are under the king's dominion obey him, andfall away every one from the religion of their fathers, and giveconsent to his commandments:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	20	Yet will I and my sons and my brethren walk in the covenantof our fathers.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	21	God forbid that we should forsake the law and the ordinances.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	22	We will not hearken to the king's words, to go from ourreligion, either on the right hand, or the left.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	23	Now when he had left speaking these words, there came one ofthe Jews in the sight of all to sacrifice on the altar which wasat Modin, according to the king's commandment.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	24	Which thing when Mattathias saw, he was inflamed with zeal,and his reins trembled, neither could he forbear to shew hisanger according to judgment: wherefore he ran, and slew him uponthe altar.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	25	Also the king's commissioner, who compelled men to sacrifice,he killed at that time, and the altar he pulled down.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	26	Thus dealt he zealously for the law of God like as Phineesdid unto Zambri the son of Salom.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	27	And Mattathias cried throughout the city with a loud voice,saying, Whosoever is zealous of the law, and maintaineth thecovenant, let him follow me.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	28	So he and his sons fled into the mountains, and left all thatever they had in the city.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	29	Then many that sought after justice and judgment went downinto the wilderness, to dwell there:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	30	Both they, and their children, and their wives; and theircattle; because afflictions increased sore upon them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	31	Now when it was told the king's servants, and the host thatwas at Jerusalem, in the city of David, that certain men, whohad broken the king's commandment, were gone down into thesecret places in the wilderness,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	32	They pursued after them a great number, and having overtakenthem, they camped against them, and made war against them on thesabbath day.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	33	And they said unto them, Let that which ye have done hithertosuffice; come forth, and do according to the commandment of theking, and ye shall live.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	34	But they said, We will not come forth, neither will we do theking's commandment, to profane the sabbath day.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	35	So then they gave them the battle with all speed.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	36	Howbeit they answered them not, neither cast they a stone atthem, nor stopped the places where they lay hid;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	37	But said, Let us die all in our innocency: heaven and earthwill testify for us, that ye put us to death wrongfully.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	38	So they rose up against them in battle on the sabbath, andthey slew them, with their wives and children and their cattle,to the number of a thousand people.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	39	Now when Mattathias and his friends understood hereof, theymourned for them right sore.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	40	And one of them said to another, If we all do as our brethrenhave done, and fight not for our lives and laws against theheathen, they will now quickly root us out of the earth.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	41	At that time therefore they decreed, saying, Whosoever shallcome to make battle with us on the sabbath day, we will fightagainst him; neither will we die all, as our brethren that weremurdered im the secret places.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	42	Then came there unto him a company of Assideans who weremighty men of Israel, even all such as were voluntarily devotedunto the law.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	43	Also all they that fled for persecution joined themselvesunto them, and were a stay unto them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	44	So they joined their forces, and smote sinful men in theiranger, and wicked men in their wrath: but the rest fled to theheathen for succour.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	45	Then Mattathias and his friends went round about, and pulleddown the altars:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	46	And what children soever they found within the coast ofIsrael uncircumcised, those they circumcised valiantly.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	47	They pursued also after the proud men, and the work prosperedin their hand.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	48	So they recovered the law out of the hand of the Gentiles,and out of the hand of kings, neither suffered they the sinnerto triumph.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	49	Now when the time drew near that Mattathias should die, hesaid unto his sons, Now hath pride and rebuke gotten strength,and the time of destruction, and the wrath of indignation:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	50	Now therefore, my sons, be ye zealous for the law, and giveyour lives for the covenant of your fathers.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	51	Call to remembrance what acts our fathers did in their time;so shall ye receive great honour and an everlasting name.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	52	Was not Abraham found faithful in temptation, and it wasimputed unto him for righteousness?

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	62	Fear not then the words of a sinful man: for his glory shallbe dung and worms.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	63	To day he shall be lifted up and to morrow he shall not befound, because he is returned into his dust, and his thought iscome to nothing.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	64	Wherefore, ye my sons, be valiant and shew yourselves men inthe behalf of the law; for by it shall ye obtain glory.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	65	And behold, I know that your brother Simon is a man ofcounsel, give ear unto him alway: he shall be a father unto you.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	66	As for Judas Maccabeus, he hath been mighty and strong, evenfrom his youth up: let him be your captain, and fight the battleof the people.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	67	Take also unto you all those that observe the law, and avengeye the wrong of your people.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	2	69	So he blessed them, and was gathered to his fathers.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	2	And all his brethren helped him, and so did all they thatheld with his father, and they fought with cheerfulness thebattle of Israel.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	3	So he gat his people great honour, and put on a breastplateas a giant, and girt his warlike harness about him, and he madebattles, protecting the host with his sword.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	4	In his acts he was like a lion, and like a lion's whelproaring for his prey.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	5	For He pursued the wicked, and sought them out, and burnt upthose that vexed his people.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	12	Wherefore Judas took their spoils, and Apollonius' swordalso, and therewith he fought all his life long.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	15	So he made him ready to go up, and there went with him amighty host of the ungodly to help him, and to be avenged of thechildren of Israel.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	16	And when he came near to the going up of Bethhoron, Judaswent forth to meet him with a small company:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	17	Who, when they saw the host coming to meet them, said untoJudas, How shall we be able, being so few, to fight against sogreat a multitude and so strong, seeing we are ready to faintwith fasting all this day?
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	18	Unto whom Judas answered, It is no hard matter for many to beshut up in the hands of a few; and with the God of heaven it isall one, to deliver with a great multitude, or a small company:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	19	For the victory of battle standeth not in the multitude of anhost; but strength cometh from heaven.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	28	He opened also his treasure, and gave his soldiers pay for ayear, commanding them to be ready whensoever he should needthem.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	29	Nevertheless, when he saw that the money of his treasuresfailed and that the tributes in the country were small, becauseof the dissension and plague, which he had brought upon the landin taking away the laws which had been of old time;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	30	He feared that he should not be able to bear the charges anylonger, nor to have such gifts to give so liberally as he didbefore: for he had abounded above the kings that were beforehim.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	3	31	Wherefore, being greatly perplexed in his mind, he determinedto go into Persia, there to take the tributes of the countries,and to gather much money.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	26	Now all the strangers that had escaped came and told Lysiaswhat had happened:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	27	Who, when he heard thereof, was confounded and discouraged,because neither such things as he would were done unto Israel,nor such things as the king commanded him were come to pass.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	28	The next year therefore following Lysias gathered togetherthreescore thousand choice men of foot, and five thousandhorsemen, that he might subdue them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	29	So they came into Idumea, and pitched their tents atBethsura, and Judas met them with ten thousand men.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	30	And when he saw that mighty army, he prayed and said, Blessedart thou, O Saviour of Israel, who didst quell the violence ofthe mighty man by the hand of thy servant David, and gavest thehost of strangers into the hands of Jonathan the son of Saul,and his armourbearer;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	31	Shut up this army in the hand of thy people Israel, and letthem be confounded in their power and horsemen:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	32	Make them to be of no courage, and cause the boldness oftheir strength to fall away, and let them quake at theirdestruction:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	33	Cast them down with the sword of them that love thee, and letall those that know thy name praise thee with thanksgiving.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	34	So they joined battle; and there were slain of the host ofLysias about five thousand men, even before them were theyslain.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	35	Now when Lysias saw his army put to flight, and the manlinessof Judas' soldiers, and how they were ready either to live ordie valiantly, he went into Antiochia, and gathered together acompany of strangers, and having made his army greater than itwas, he purposed to come again into Judea.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	36	Then said Judas and his brethren, Behold, our enemies arediscomfited: let us go up to cleanse and dedicate the sanctuary.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	37	Upon this all the host assembled themselves together, andwent up into mount Sion.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	38	And when they saw the sanctuary desolate, and the altarprofaned, and the gates burned up, and shrubs growing in thecourts as in a forest, or in one of the mountains, yea, and thepriests' chambers pulled down;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	39	They rent their clothes, and made great lamentation, and castashes upon their heads,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	40	And fell down flat to the ground upon their faces, and blewan alarm with the trumpets, and cried toward heaven.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	41	Then Judas appointed certain men to fight against those thatwere in the fortress, until he had cleansed the sanctuary.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	42	So he chose priests of blameless conversation, such as hadpleasure in the law:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	43	Who cleansed the sanctuary, and bare out the defiled stonesinto an unclean place.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	44	And when as they consulted what to do with the altar of burntofferings, which was profaned;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	45	They thought it best to pull it down, lest it should be areproach to them, because the heathen had defiled it: whereforethey pulled it down,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	46	And laid up the stones in the mountain of the temple in aconvenient place, until there should come a prophet to shew whatshould be done with them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	47	Then they took whole stones according to the law, and built anew altar according to the former;
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	48	And made up the sanctuary, and the things that were withinthe temple, and hallowed the courts.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	49	They made also new holy vessels, and into the temple theybrought the candlestick, and the altar of burnt offerings, andof incense, and the table.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	50	And upon the altar they burned incense, and the lamps thatwere upon the candlestick they lighted, that they might givelight in the temple.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	51	Furthermore they set the loaves upon the table, and spreadout the veils, and finished all the works which they had begunto make.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	52	Now on the five and twentieth day of the ninth month, whichis called the month Casleu, in the hundred forty and eighthyear, they rose up betimes in the morning,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	53	And offered sacrifice according to the law upon the new altarof burnt offerings, which they had made.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	54	Look, at what time and what day the heathen had profaned it,even in that was it dedicated with songs, and citherns, andharps, and cymbals.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	55	Then all the people fell upon their faces, worshipping andpraising the God of heaven, who had given them good success.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	56	And so they kept the dedication of the altar eight days andoffered burnt offerings with gladness, and sacrificed thesacrifice of deliverance and praise.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	57	They decked also the forefront of the temple with crowns ofgold, and with shields; and the gates and the chambers theyrenewed, and hanged doors upon them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	58	Thus was there very great gladness among the people, for thatthe reproach of the heathen was put away.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	59	Moreover Judas and his brethren with the whole congregationof Israel ordained, that the days of the dedication of the altarshould be kept in their season from year to year by the space ofeight days, from the five and twentieth day of the month Casleu,with mirth and gladness.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	60	At that time also they builded up the mount Sion with highwalls and strong towers round about, lest the Gentiles shouldcome and tread it down as they had done before.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	4	61	And they set there a garrison to keep it, and fortifiedBethsura to preserve it; that the people might have a defenceagainst Idumea.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	1	Now when the nations round about heard that the altar wasbuilt and the sanctuary renewed as before, it displeased themvery much.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	2	Wherefore they thought to destroy the generation of Jacobthat was among them, and thereupon they began to slay anddestroy the people.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	3	Then Judas fought against the children of Esau in Idumea atArabattine, because they besieged Gael: and he gave them a greatoverthrow, and abated their courage, and took their spoils.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	4	Also he remembered the injury of the children of Bean, whohad been a snare and an offence unto the people, in that theylay in wait for them in the ways.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	5	He shut them up therefore in the towers, and encamped againstthem, and destroyed them utterly, and burned the towers of thatplace with fire, and all that were therein.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	6	Afterward he passed over to the children of Ammon, where hefound a mighty power, and much people, with Timotheus theircaptain.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	7	So he fought many battles with them, till at length they werediscomfited before him; and he smote them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	8	And when he had taken Jazar, with the towns belongingthereto, he returned into Judea.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	9	Then the heathen that were at Galaad assembled themselvestogether against the Israelites that were in their quarters, todestroy them; but they fled to the fortress of Dathema.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	10	And sent letters unto Judas and his brethren, The heathenthat are round about us are assembled together against us todestroy us:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	11	And they are preparing to come and take the fortresswhereunto we are fled, Timotheus being captain of their host.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	12	Come now therefore, and deliver us from their hands, for manyof us are slain:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	13	Yea, all our brethren that were in the places of Tobie areput to death: their wives and their children also they havecarried away captives, and borne away their stuff; and they havedestroyed there about a thousand men.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	14	While these letters were yet reading, behold, there cameother messengers from Galilee with their clothes rent, whoreported on this wise,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	15	And said, They of Ptolemais, and of Tyrus, and Sidon, and allGalilee of the Gentiles, are assembled together against us toconsume us.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	16	Now when Judas and the people heard these words, thereassembled a great congregation together, to consult what theyshould do for their brethren, that were in trouble, andassaulted of them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	17	Then said Judas unto Simon his brother, Choose thee out men,and go and deliver thy brethren that are in Galilee, for I andJonathan my brother will go into the country of Galaad.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	18	So he left Joseph the son of Zacharias, and Azarias, captainsof the people, with the remnant of the host in Judea to keep it.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	19	Unto whom he gave commandment, saying, Take ye the charge ofthis people, and see that ye make not war against the heathenuntil the time that we come again.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	20	Now unto Simon were given three thousand men to go intoGalilee, and unto Judas eight thousand men for the country ofGalaad.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	21	Then went Simon into Galilee, where he fought many battleswith the heathen, so that the heathen were discomfited by him.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	22	And he pursued them unto the gate of Ptolemais; and therewere slain of the heathen about three thousand men, whose spoilshe took.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	23	And those that were in Galilee, and in Arbattis, with theirwives and their children, and all that they had, took he awaywith him, and brought them into Judea with great joy.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	24	Judas Maccabeus also and his brother Jonathan went overJordan, and travelled three days' journey in the wilderness,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	25	Where they met with the Nabathites, who came unto them in apeaceable manner, and told them every thing that had happened totheir brethren in the land of Galaad:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	26	And how that many of them were shut up in Bosora, and Bosor,and Alema, Casphor, Maked, and Carnaim; all these cities arestrong and great:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	27	And that they were shut up in the rest of the cities of thecountry of Galaad, and that against to morrow they had appointedto bring their host against the forts, and to take them, and todestroy them all in one day.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	28	Hereupon Judas and his host turned suddenly by the way of thewilderness unto Bosora; and when he had won the city, he slewall the males with the edge of the sword, and took all theirspoils, and burned the city with fire,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	29	From whence he removed by night, and went till he came to thefortress.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	30	And betimes in the morning they looked up, and, behold, therewas an innumerable people bearing ladders and other engines ofwar, to take the fortress: for they assaulted them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	31	When Judas therefore saw that the battle was begun, and thatthe cry of the city went up to heaven, with trumpets, and agreat sound,
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	32	He said unto his host, Fight this day for your brethren.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	33	So he went forth behind them in three companies, who soundedtheir trumpets, and cried with prayer.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	34	Then the host of Timotheus, knowing that it was Maccabeus,fled from him: wherefore he smote them with a great slaughter;so that there were killed of them that day about eight thousandmen.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	38	So Judas sent men to espy the host, who brought him word,saying, All the heathen that be round about us are assembledunto them, even a very great host.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	39	He hath also hired the Arabians to help them and they havepitched their tents beyond the brook, ready to come and fightagainst thee. Upon this Judas went to meet them.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	40	Then Timotheus said unto the captains of his host, When Judasand his host come near the brook, if he pass over first unto us,we shall not be able to withstand him; for he will mightilyprevail against us:
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	41	But if he be afraid, and camp beyond the river, we shall goover unto him, and prevail against him.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	42	Now when Judas came near the brook, he caused the scribes ofthe people to remain by the brook: unto whom he gavecommandment, saying, Suffer no man to remain in the camp, butlet all come to the battle.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	43	So he went first over unto them, and all the people afterhim: then all the heathen, being discomfited before him, castaway their weapons, and fled unto the temple that was atCarnaim.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	46	Now when they came unto Ephron, (this was a great city in theway as they should go, very well fortified) they could not turnfrom it, either on the right hand or the left, but must needspass through the midst of it.

The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	60	And so it was, that Joseph and Azaras were put to flight, andpursued unto the borders of Judea: and there were slain that dayof the people of Israel about two thousand men.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	61	Thus was there a great overthrow among the children ofIsrael, because they were not obedient unto Judas and hisbrethren, but thought to do some valiant act.
The First Book of The Maccabees	1Mac	5	62	Moreover these men came not of the seed of those, by whosehand deliverance was given unto Israel.
